śrīśrībhaktirasāmṛtasindhuḥ bhagavadbhaktibhedanirūpakaḥpūrvavibhāgaḥ sāmānyabhaktiḥprathamalaharīśrīśrīrādhāgovindadevau vijayeteakhilarasāmṛtamūrtiḥ prasṛmararuciruddhatārakāpāliḥ kalitaśyāmālalito rādhāpreyān vidhur jayati  RBhrs hṛdi yasya preraṇayā pravartito haṃ varākarūpo pi tasya hareḥ padakamalaṃ vande caitanyadevasya  RBhrs viśrāmamandiratyā tasya sanātanatanor madīśasya bhaktirasāmṛtasindhur bhavatu sadāyam pramodāya  RBhrs bhaktirasāmṛtasindhau carataḥ paribhūtakālajālabhiyaḥ bhaktamakarān aśīlitamuktinadīkān namasāmi  RBhrs mīmāṃsakabaḍavāgneḥ kaṭhinām api kuṇṭhayann asau sphuratu sanātana suciraṃ tava bhaktirasāmṛtāmbhodhiḥ  RBhrs bhaktirasasya prastutir akhilajagaṅmaṅgalaprasaṅgasya ajñenāpi mayāsya kriyate suhṛdām pramodāya  RBhrs etasya bhagavadbhaktirasāmṛtapayonidheḥ catvārah khalu vakṣyante bhāgāḥ pūrvādayaḥ kramāt  RBhrs tatra pūrve vibhāge smin bhaktibhedanirūpake anukrameṇa vaktavyaṃ laharīṇāṃ catuṣṭayam  RBhrs ādyā sāmānyabhaktyāḍhyā dvitīyā sādhanānvitā bhāvāśritā tṛtīyā ca turyā premanirūpikā  RBhrs tatrādau suṣṭhu vaiśiṣṭyam asyāḥ kathayituṃ sphuṭam lakṣaṇaṃ kriyate bhakter uttamāyāḥ satāṃ matam  RBhrs anyābhilāṣitāśūnyaṃ jñānakarmādyanāvṛtam ānukūlyena kṛṣṇānuśīlanaṃ bhaktir uttamā  RBhrs yathā śrīnāradapañcarātresarvopādhivinirmuktaṃ tatparatvena nirmalam hṛṣīkeṇa hṛṣīkeśasevanaṃ bhaktir ucyate  RBhrs śrībhāgavatasya tṛtīyaskandhe ca ahaituky avyavahitā yā bhaktiḥ puruṣottame  RBhrs sālokyasārṣṭisāmīpyasārūpyaikatvam apy uta dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇanti vinā matsevanaṃ janāḥ  RBhrs sa eva bhaktiyogākhya ātyantika udāhṛtaḥ  RBhrs sālokyetyādipadyasthabhaktotkarṣaṇirūpaṇam bhakter viśuddhatāvyaktyā lakṣaṇe paryavasyati  RBhrs kleśaghnī śubhadā mokṣalaghutākṛt sudurlabhā sāndrānandaviśeṣātmā śrīkṛṣṇākarṣiṇī ca sā  RBhrs tatrāsyāḥ kleśaghnatvam kleśās tu pāpaṃ tadbījam avidyā ceti te tridhā  RBhrs tatra pāpamaprārabdhaṃ bhavet pāpaṃ prārabdhaṃ ceti tad dvidhā  RBhrs tatra aprārabdhaharatvamyathā ekaḍaśe yathāgniḥ susamiddhārciḥ karoty edhāṃsi bhasmasāt tathā madviṣayābhaktir uddhavaināṃsi kṛtsnaśaḥ  RBhrs prārabdhaharatvamyathā tṛtīye yannāmadheyaśravaṇānukīrtanādyatprahvaṇad yatsmaraṇād api kvacit śvādo pi sadyaḥ savanāya kalpatekutaḥ punas te bhagavan nu darśanāt  RBhrs durjātir eva savanāyogyatve kāraṇam matam durjātyārambhakaṃ pāpaṃ yat syāt prārabdham eva tat  RBhrs padmapurāne caaprārabdhaphalaṃ pāpaṃ kūṭaṃ bījaṃ phalonmukham krameṇaiva pralīyeta viṣṇubhaktiratātmanām  RBhrs bījaharatvamyathā ṣaṣṭhe tais tāny aghāni sarvajagatām anuraktatā sadguṇāḥ sukham ityādīny ākhyātāni manīṣibhiḥ  RBhrs tatra jagatprīṇanādidvayapradatvamyathā pādmeyenārcito haris tena tarpitāni jaganty api rajyanti jantavas tatra jangamāḥ sthāvarā api  RBhrs sadguṇādipradatvamyathā pañcame yasyāsti bhaktir bhagavaty akiñcanāsarvair guṇais tatra samāsate surāḥ harāv abhaktasya kuto mahadguṇāmanorathenāsati dhāvato bahiḥ  RBhrs sukhapradatvamsukhaṃ vaiṣayikaṃ brāhmam aiśvaraṃ ceti tat tridhā  RBhrs yathā tantresiddhayaḥ paramāścaryā bhuktir muktiś ca śāśvatī nityaṃ ca paramānando bhaved govindabhaktitaḥ  RBhrs yathā haribhaktisudhodaye cabhūyo pi yāce deveśa tvayi bhaktir dṛḍhāstu me yā mokṣāntacaturvarga phaladā sukhadā latā  RBhrs mokṣalaghutākṛtmanāg eva prarūḍhāyāṃ hṛdaye bhagavādratau puruṣārthās tu catvārās saptame  ca nāradoktauyūyaṃ nṛloke bata bhūribhāgālokaṃ punānā munayo bhiyanti yeṣāṃ gṛhān āvasatīti sākṣādguḍhaṃ paraṃ brahma manuṣyaliṅgam  RBhrs agrato vakṣyamāṇāyās tridhā bhakter anukramāt dviśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ padair etan māhātyaṃ parikīrtitam  RBhrs kiṃ casvalpāpi rucir eva syād bhaktitattvāvabodhikā yuktis tu kevalā naiva yad asyā apratiṣṭhatā  RBhrs tatra prācīnair apy uktamyatnenāpādito py arthaḥ kuśalair anumātṛbhiḥ abhiyuktatarair anyair anyathaivopapādyate  RBhrs iti śrī śrī bhaktirasāmṛtasindhaupūrvabhāge bhaktisāmānya laharī prathamā dvitīyā laharīsādhanabhaktiḥsā bhaktiḥ sādhanaṃ devarṣiṇoditā  RBhrs yathā saptame tasmāt kenāpy upāyena manaḥ kṛṣṇe niveśayet  RBhrs  iti vaidhī rāgānugā ceti sā dvidhā sādhanābhidhā  RBhrs tatra vaidhīyatra rāgānavāptatvāt pravṛttir upajāyate śāsanenaiva śāstrasya sā vaidhī bhaktir ucyate  RBhrs yatha dvitīye tasmād bhārata sarvātmā bhagavān īśvaro hariḥ śrotavyaḥ kīrtitavyaś ca smartavyaś cecchatābhayam  RBhrs pādme casmartavyaḥ satataṃ viṣṇur vismartavyo na jātucit sarve vidhiniṣedhāḥ syur etayor eva kiṅkarāḥ  RBhrs ity asau syād vidhir nityaḥ sarvavarṇāśramādiṣu nityatve py asya nirṇītam ekādaśyādivatphalam  RBhrs yathā ekādāśe tu vyaktam evoktammukha bāhūrupādebhyaḥ puruṣasyāśramaiḥ saha catvāro jajñire varṇā guṇair viprādayaḥ pṛthak  RBhrs ya eṣāṃ puruṣaṃ sākṣād ātmaprabhavam īśvaram na bhajanty avajānanti sthānād bhraṣṭāḥ patanty adhaḥ  RBhrs tat phalaṃ ca tatraiva evaṃ kriyāyogapathaiḥ pumān vaidikatāntrikaiḥ arcann ubhyataḥ siddhiṃ matto vindaty abhīpsitām  RBhrs pañcarātre casurarṣe vihitā śāstre harim uddiśya yā nigadyate  RBhrs tatra gītādiṣūktānāṃ caturṇām adhikāriṇām madhye yasmin bhagavatah kṛpā syāt tatpriyasya vā  RBhrs sa kṣīṇatattadbhāvaḥ syāc chuddhabhaktyadhikāravān yathebhaḥ śaunakādiś ca dhruvaḥ sa ca catuḥsanaḥ  RBhrs bhuktimuktispṛhā yāvat piśācī hṛdi vartate tāvad bhaktisukhasyātra katham abhyudayo bhavet  RBhrs tatrāpi ca viśeṣeṇa gatim aṇvīm anicchataḥ bhaktir hṛtamanaḥprāṇān premṇā tān RBhrs tatraiva sālokyasārṣṭisāmīpya sārūpyaikatvam apy uta dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇanti vinā matsevanaṃ janāḥ  RBhrs caturthe śrīdhruvoktau yā nirvṛtis tanubhṛtāṃ tava pādapadmadhyānād vāsamañjasa tvā virahayya kāṅkṣe  RBhrs tatraiva śrīrudroktau nārāyaṇaparāḥ sarve na kutaścana bibhyati svargāpavarganarakeṣv api tulyārthadarśinaḥ  RBhrs tatraiva indroktau ārādhanaṃ bhagavata īhamānā nirāśiṣaḥ ye tu necchanty api paraṃ te svārthakuśalāḥ smṛtāḥ  RBhrs saptame prahlādoktau tuṣṭe ca tatra kim alabhyam ananta ādyekiṃ tair guṇavyatikarād iha ye svasiddhāḥ dharmādayaḥ kim aguṇena ca kāṅkṣitenasāraṃ juṣāṃ caraṇayor upagāyatāṃ naḥ  RBhrs tatraiva śakroktau pratyānītāḥ parama bhavatā trāyatā naḥ svabhāgādaityākrāntaṃ hṛdayakamalaṃ tadgṛhaṃ pratyabodhi kālagrastaṃ kiyad idam aho nātha śuśrūṣatāṃ temuktis teṣāṃ na hi bahumatā nārasiṃhāparaiḥ kim  RBhrs aṣṭame śrīgajendroktau ekāntino yasya na kañcanārthaṃvāñchanti ye vai bhagavatprapannāḥ atyadbhutaṃ taccaritaṃ sumaṅgalaṃgāyanta ānandasamudramagnāḥ  RBhrs navame śrīvaikuṇṭhanāthoktau matsevayā pratītaṃ te sālokyādicatuṣṭayam necchanti sevayā pūrṇāḥ kuto nyat kālaviplutam  RBhrs śrīdaśame nāgapatnīstutau na nākapṛṣṭhaṃ na ca sārvabhaumaṃna pārameṣṭhyaṃ na rasādhipatyam na yogasiddhīr apunarbhavaṃ vāvāñchanti yatpādarajaḥprapannāḥ  RBhrs tatraiva śrīvedastutau duravagamātmatattvanigamāya vinānyat  RBhrs dvādaśe śrīrudroktau naivecchaty āśiṣaḥ kvāpi brahmarṣir mokṣam apy uta bhaktiṃ parāṃ bhagavati labdhavān puruṣe vyaye  RBhrs padmapurāṇe ca kārttikamāhātmye dāmodarāṣṭakevaraṃ deva ataeva śrībhāgavate ṣaṣṭhe muktānām api siddhānāṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ sudurlabhaḥ praśāntātmā koṭiṣv api mahāmune  RBhrs prathame ca śrīdharmarājamātuḥ stutau tathā paramahaṃsānāṃ munīnām amalātmanām abhede pi śrīśakṛṣṇasvarūpayoḥ rasenotkṛṣyate kṛṣṇarūpam eṣā rasasthitiḥ  RBhrs śāstrataḥ śrūyate bhaktau nṛmātrasyādhikāritā sarvādhikāritāṃ māghasnānasya bruvatā yataḥ dṛṣtāntitā vaśiṣṭhena sambabhuḥ  RBhrs api caananuṣṭhānato doṣo bhaktyaṅgānāṃ prajāyate na karmaṇām akaraṇād eṣa bhaktyadhikāriṇām  RBhrs niṣiddhācārato daivāt prāyaścittaṃ tu nocitam iti vaiṣṇavaśāstrāṇāṃ rahasyaṃ tadvidāṃ matam  RBhrs yathaikādaśe  sve sve dhikāre yā niṣṭhā sā guṇaḥ parikīrtitaḥ viparyayas tu doṣaḥ syād ubhayor eṣa niścayaḥ  RBhrs prathame tyaktvā svadharmaṃ caraṇāmbujam harerbhajann apakvo tha patet tato yadi yatra kva vābhadram abhūd amuṣya kiṃko vārtha āpto bhajatāṃ svadharmataḥ  RBhrs ekādaśe ājñāyaiva guṇān doṣān mayādiṣṭān api svakān dharmān santyajya yaḥ sarvān māṃ bhajet sa ca sattamaḥ  RBhrs tatraiva devarṣibhūtāptanṝṇāṃ pitṝṇāṃna kiṅkaro nāyam ṛṇī ca rājan sarvātmanā yaḥ śaraṇaṃ śaraṇyaṃgato mukundaṃ parihṛtya kartam  RBhrs śrībhagavadgītāsu sarvadharman parityājya mām ekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ahaṃ tvāṃ sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā sucaḥ  RBhrs agastyasaṃhitāyāmyathā vidhiniṣedhau tu muktaṃ naivopasarpataḥ tathā na spṛśato rāmopāsakaṃ vidhipūrvakam  RBhrs ekādaśe eva svapādamulaṃ bhajataḥ priyasyatyaktāny abhāvasya hariḥ pareśaḥ vikarma yac cotpatitaṃ kathañciddhunoti sarvaṃ hṛdi sanniviṣṭaḥ  RBhrs haribhaktivilāse syā bhakter aṅgāni lakṣaśaḥ kintu tāni prasiddhāni nirdiśyante yathāmati  RBhrs atra aṅgalakṣaṇam āśritāvāntarānekabhedaṃ kevalam eva vā ekaṃ karmātra vidvadbhir ekaṃ bhaktyaṅgam ucyate  RBhrs atha aṅgānigurupādāśrayas tasmāt kṛṣṇadīkṣādiśikṣaṇam viśrambheṇa guroḥ sevā sādhuvartmānuvartanam  RBhrs saddharmapṛcchā bhogādityāgaḥ kṛṣṇasya hetave nivāso dvārakādau ca gaṅgāder api sannidhau  RBhrs vyāvahāreṣu sarveṣu mahārambhādyanudyamaḥ  RBhrs bahugranthakalābhyāsavyākhyāvādavivarjanam  RBhrs vyāvahāre py akārpaṇyaṃ śokādyavaśavartitā  RBhrs anyadevān avajñā ca bhūtānudvegadāyitā sevānāmāparādhānām udbhavābhāvakāritā  RBhrs kṛṣṇatadbhaktavidveṣavinindādyasahiṣṇutā vyatirekatayāmīṣāṃ daśānāṃ syād anuṣṭhitīḥ  RBhrs asyās tatra praveśāya dvāratve py aṅgaviṃśateḥ trayāṃ pradhānam evoktaṃ gurupādāśrayādikam  RBhrs dhṛtir vaiṣṇavacihṇānāṃ harer nāmākṣarasya ca nirmālyādeś ca tasyāgre tāṇḍavaṃ daṇḍavannatiḥ  RBhrs abhyutthānam anuvrajyā gatiḥ sthāne parikramaḥ arcanaṃ paricaryā ca gītaṃ saṅkīrtanaṃ japaḥ  RBhrs vijñaptiḥ stavapāṭhaś ca svādo naivedyapādyayoḥ dhūpamālyādisaurabhyaṃ śrīmūrteḥ spṛṣṭir īkṣaṇam  RBhrs ārātrikotsavādeś ca śravaṇaṃ tatkṛpekṣaṇam smṛtir dhyānaṃ tathā dāsyaṃ sakhyam ātmanivedanam  RBhrs nijapriyopaharaṇaṃ tadarthe khilaceṣṭitam sarvathā śaraṇāpattis tadīyānāṃ ca sevanam  RBhrs tadīyās tulasīśāstramathurāvaiṣṇavādayaḥ yathāvaibhavasāmagrī sadgoṣṭhībhir mahotsavaḥ  RBhrs ūrjādaro viśeṣeṇa yātrā janmadinādiṣu śraddhā viśeṣataḥ prītiḥ śrīmūrter aṅghrisevane  RBhrs śrīmadbhāgavatārthānām āsvādo rasikaiḥ saha sajātīyāśaye snigdhe sādhau saṅgaḥ svato vare  RBhrs nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ śrīmathurāmaṇḍale sthitiḥ  RBhrs aṅgānāṃ pañcakasyāsya pūrvaṃ vilikhitasya ca nikhilaśraiṣṭhyabodhāya punar apy atra kīrtanam  RBhrs iti kāyahṛṣīkāntaḥkaraṇānām upāsanāḥ  RBhrs catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ pṛthak sāṅghātikabhedāt kramādināḥ  RBhrs athārṣānumatenaiṣām udāharaṇam īryate  RBhrs   tatra gurupādāśrayoyathā ekādaśe tasmād guruṃ prapadyeta jijñāsuḥ śreya uttamam śābde pare ca sevāyathā tatraiva ācāryaṃ māṃ vijānīyān nāvamanyeta karhicit na martyabuddhyāsūyeta sarvadevamayo guruḥ  RBhrs   sādhuvartmānuvartanamyathā skāndesa mṛgyaḥ śreyasāṃ hetuḥ panthāḥ santāpavarjitaḥ anvāptaśramaṃ pūrve yena santaḥ pratasthire  RBhrs brahmayāmale caśrutismṛtipurāṇādipañcarātravidhiṃ vinā aikāntikī harer bhaktir utpātāyaiva kalpate  RBhrs bhaktir aikāntikī veyam avicārāt pratīyate gaṅgādivāsoyathā prathame yā vai lasacchrītulasīvimiśrakṛṣṇāṅghrireṇvabhyadhikāmbunetrī punāti seśān ubhayatra lokānkas tāṃ na seveta mariṣyamāṇaḥ  RBhrs  yāvadarthānuvartitāyathā nāradīyeyāvatā syāt nānādevaikasevinām  RBhrs       śiṣyānanubanddhitvāditrayaṃyathā saptame na śiṣyān anubadhnīta granthān naivābhyased bahūn na vyākhyām upayuñjīta nārambhān ārabhet kvacit  RBhrs   vyāvahāre py akārpaṇyaṃyathā pādmealabdhe vā vinaṣṭe vā bhakṣyācchādanasādhane aviklavamatir bhūtvā harim eva dhiyā smaret  RBhrs  śokādyavaśavartitāyathā tatraivaśokāmarṣādibhir bhāvair ākrāntaṃ yasya mānasam kathaṃ tatra mukundasya sphūrtisambhāvanā bhavet  RBhrs  anyadevānajñāyathā tatraivaharir eva sadārādhyaḥ sarvadeveśvareśvaraḥ itare brahmarudrādyā nāvajñeyāḥ kadācana  RBhrs  bhūtānudvegadāyitāyathā anuvrajyā yathā bhaviṣyottarerathena saha gacchanti pārśvataḥ pṛṣṭhato grataḥ viṣṇunaiva samāḥ sarve bhavanti śvapadādayaḥ  RBhrs   sthāne gatiḥsthānaṃ tīrthaṃ gṛhaṃ cāsya tatra tīrthe gatir yathā atha japaḥmantrasya sulaghūccāro japa ity abhidhīyate  RBhrs yathā pādmekṛṣṇāya nama ity eṣa mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ bhaktānāṃ japatāṃ bhūpa svargamokṣaphalapradaḥ  RBhrs   atha vijñaptiḥyathā RBhrs tatra samprārthanātmikāyathā pādmeyuvatīnāṃ yathā yūni yūnāṃ ca yuvatau yathā mano bhiramate tadvan mano bhiramatāṃ tvayi  RBhrs dainyabodhikāyathā tatraivamattulyo nāsti pāpātmā nāparādhī ca sa dāyabhāk  RBhrs atha smṛtiḥyathā kathaṃ cinmanasā sambandhaḥ smṛtir ucyate  RBhrs yathā viṣṇupurāṇe smṛte sakalakalyāṇabhājanaṃ yatra jāyate puruṣaṃ tam ajaṃ nityaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ harim  RBhrs yathā ca pādmeprayāṇe cāprayāṇe ca yannāma smaratāṃ nṝṇām sadyo naśyati pāpaugho namas tasmai cidātmane  RBhrs atha dhyānamdhyānam rupaguṇakrīḍāsevādeḥ suṣṭhu cintanam  RBhrs tatra rūpadhyānaṃyathā apīśvare bhaved bhāgavato dharmas tatkarma kimutārpitam  RBhrs karma svābhāvikaṃ bhadraṃ japadhyānārcanādi ca itīdaṃ dvividhaṃ kṛṣṇe vaiṣṇavair dāsyam arpitam  RBhrs mṛduśraddhasya kathitā svalpā karmādhikāritā tadarpitaṃ harau dāsyam iti kaiścid udīryate  RBhrs dvitiyaṃ yathā nāradīyeīhā yasya harer dāsye karmaṇā manasā girā nikhilāsv apy avasthāsu jīvanmuktaḥ sa ucyate  RBhrs atha sakhyamviśvāso mitravṛttiś ca sakhyaṃ dvividham īritam  RBhrs tatra ādyaṃyathā mahābhāratepratijñā tava govinda na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati iti saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya prāṇān saṃdhārayāmy aham  RBhrs tathā ekādaśe  catribhuvanavibhavahetave py akuṇṭhasmṛtir ajitātmasurādibhir vimṛgyāt na calati bhagavatpadāravindāllavanimiṣārdham api yaḥ sa vaiṣṇavāgryaḥ  RBhrs śraddhāmātrasya tadbhaktāv adhikāritvahetutā aṅgatvam asya viśvāsaviśeṣasya tu keśave  RBhrs dvitīyaṃ yathā agastyasaṃhitāyāmparicaryā parāḥ kecit prāsādeṣu ca śerate manuṣyam iva taṃ draṣṭuṃ vyāvahartuṃ ca bandhuvat  RBhrs rāgānugāṅgatāsya syād vidhimārgānapekṣatvāt mārgadvayena caitena sādhyā sakhyaratir matā  RBhrs atha ātmanivedanaṃyathā ekādaśe martyo yadā tyaktasamastakarmāniveditātmā vicikīrṣito me tadāmṛtatvaṃ pratipadyamānomayātmabhuūyāyā ca kalpate vai  RBhrs artho dvidhātmaśabdasya paṇḍitair upapāyate dehyahantāspadaṃ kaiścid dehaḥ kaiścin mamatvabhāk  RBhrs tatra dehī yathā yāmunācāryastotre vapurādiṣu yo pi ko pi vāguṇato sāni yathā tathāvidhaḥ tad ayaṃ tava pādapadmayoraham adyaiva mayā samarpitaḥ  RBhrs deho yathā bhaktivivekecintāṃ kuryān na rakṣāyai vikrītasya yathā paśoḥ tathārpayan harau dehaṃ viramed asya rakṣanāt  RBhrs duṣkaratvena virale dve sakhyātmanivedane keṣāṃcid eva dhīrāṇāṃ labhate sādhanārhatām  RBhrs atha nijapriyopaharaṇaṃyathā ekādaśe yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac cātipriyam ātmanaḥ tat tan nivedayen mahyaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate  RBhrs atha tadarthe khilaceṣṭitaṃyathā pañcarātrelaukikī vaidikī vāpi yā kriyā kriyate mune harisevānukūlaiva sā kāryā bhaktim icchatā  RBhrs atha śaraṇāpattiḥyathā haribhaktivilāse tavāsmīti vadan vācā tathaiva manasā vidan tatsthānam āśritas tanvā modate śaraṇāgataḥ  RBhrs śrīnārasiṃhe catvāṃ prapanno smi śaraṇaṃ devadeva janārdana iti yaḥ śaraṇaṃ prāptas taṃ kleśād uddharāmy aham  RBhrs  atha tadīyānāṃ sevanam tulāsyaḥ yathā skāndeyā dṛṣṭā nikhilāghasaṅgaśamanī spṛṣṭā vapuḥpāvanīrogāṇām abhivanditā nirasanī siktāntakatrāsinī pratyāsattividhāyinī bhagavataḥ kṛṣṇasya saṃropitānyastā taccaraṇe vimuktiphaladā tasyai tulasyai namaḥ  RBhrs tathā ca tatraivadṛṣtā spṛṣṭā tathā dhyātā kīrtitā namitā stutā ropitā sevitā nityaṃ pūjitā tulasī śubhā  RBhrs navadhā tulasīṃ devīṃ ye bhajanti dine dine yugakoṭisahasrāṇi te vasanti harer gṛhe  RBhrs  atha śāstrasyaśāstram atra samākhyātaṃ yad bhaktipratipādakam  RBhrs yathā skāndevaiṣṇavāni tu śāstrāṇī ye śṛṇvanti paṭhanti ca dhanyās te mānavā loke tesāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prasīdati  RBhrs vaiṣṇavāni tu śāstrāṇī ye rcayanti gṛhe narāḥ sarvapāpavinirmuktā bhavanti suravanditāḥ  RBhrs tiṣṭhate vaiṣṇavaṃ śāstraṃ likhitaṃ yasya mandire tatra nārāyaṇo devaḥ svayaṃ vasati nārada  RBhrs tathā śrībhāgavate dvādaśe  casarvavedāntasāraṃ hi śrībhāgavatam iṣyate tadrasāmṛtatṛptasya nānyatra syād ratiḥ kvacit  RBhrs  atha mathurāyāḥyathā ādivārāhemathurāṃ ca parityajya yo nyatra kurute ratim mūḍho bhramati saṃsāre mohitā mama māyayā  RBhrs brahmāṇḍe catrailokyavartitīrthānāṃ sevanād durlabhā hi yā parānandamayī siddhir mathurāsparṣamātrataḥ  RBhrs śrutā smṛtā kīrtitā ca vāñchitā prekṣitā gatā spṛṣṭā śritā sevitā ca mathurābhīṣṭadā nṛṇām iti khyātaṃ purāṇeṣu na vistārabhiyocyate  RBhrs atha vaiṣṇavānāṃ sevanaṃyathā pādme ārādhanānāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ param tasmāt parataraṃ devi tadīyānāṃ samarcanam  RBhrs tṛtīye  cayatsevayā bhagavataḥ kūṭasthasya madhudviṣaḥ ratirāso bhavet tīvraḥ pādayor vyasanārdanaḥ  RBhrs skānde caśaṅkhacakrāṅkitatanuḥ śirasā mañjarīdharaḥ gopīcandanaliptāṅgo dṛṣtaś cet tadaghaṃ kutaḥ  RBhrs prathame  cayeṣāṃ saṃsmaraṇāt puṃsāṃ sadyaḥ śuddhyanti vai gṛhāḥ kiṃ punar darśanasparśapādaśaucāsanādibhiḥ  RBhrs ādīpurāṇeye me bhaktajanāḥ pārtha na me bhaktāś ca te janāḥ madbhaktānāṃ ca ye bhaktās te me bhaktatamā matāḥ  RBhrs yāvanti bhagavadbhakter aṅgāni kathitānīha prāyas tāvanti tadbhaktabhakter api budhā viduḥ  RBhrs   atha yathāvaibhavamahotsavoyathā pādmeyaḥ karoti mahīpāla harer gehe mahotsavam tasyāpi bhavati nityaṃ hariloke mahotsava  RBhrs   atha ūrjādaroyathā pādmeyathā dāmodaro bhaktavatsalo vidito janaiḥ tasyāyaṃ tādṛśo māsaḥ svalpam apy urukārakaḥ  RBhrs tatrāpi mathurāyāṃ viśeṣoyathā tatraivabhuktiṃ muktiṃ harir dadyād arcito nyatra sevinām bhaktiṃ tu na dadāty eva yato vaśyakarī hareḥ  RBhrs sā tv añjasā harer bhaktir labhyate kārttike naraiḥ mathurāyāṃ sakṛd api śrīdāmodarasevanāt  RBhrs  atha śrījanmadinayātrāyathā bhaviṣyottareyasmin dine prasūteyaṃ devakī tvāṃ janārdana taddinaṃ brūhi vaikuṇṭha kurmas te tatra cotsavam tena samyakprapannānāṃ prasādaṃ kuru keśavaḥ  RBhrs  atha śrīmūrteranghrisevane prītiḥyathā ādipurāṇemama nāmasadāgrāhī mama sevāpriyaḥ sadā bhaktis tasmai pradātavyā na tu muktiḥ kadācana  RBhrs  atha śrībhāgavatārthāsvādoyathā prathame nigamakalpatarorgalitaṃ phalaṃśukamukhād amṛtadravasaṃyutam pibata bhāgavataṃ rasam ālayaṃmuhur aho rasikā bhuvi bhāvukāḥ  RBhrs tathā dvitīye  capariniṣṭhito pi nairguṇye uttamaḥślokalīlayā gṛhitacetā rājarṣe ākhyānaṃ yad adhītavān  RBhrs atha sajātīyāśayasnigdhaśrībhagavadbhaktasaṅgoyathā prathame tulayāma lavenāpi na svargaṃ nāpunarbhavam bhagavatsaṅgisaṅgasya martyānāṃ kimutāśiṣaḥ  RBhrs haribhaktisudhodaye cayasya yatsaṅgatiḥ puṃso maṇivat syāt sa tadguṇaḥ svakūlarddhyai tato dhīmān svayūthyān eva saṃśrayet  RBhrs  atha śrīnāma saṃkīrtanaṃyathā dvitīye etan nirvidyamānānām icchatām akutobhayam yogināṃ nṛpa nirṇītaṃ harer nāmānukīrtanaṃ  RBhrs ādipurāṇe cagītvā ca mama nāmāni vicaren mama sannidhau iti bravīmi te satyaṃ krīto haṃ tasya cārjuna  RBhrs pādme cayena janmasahasrāṇi vāsudevo niṣevitaḥ tanmukhe harināmāni sadā tiṣṭhanti bhārata  RBhrs yatas tatraiva canāma cintāmaṇiḥ kṛṣṇaś caitanyarasavigrahaḥ pūrṇaḥ śuddho nityamukto bhinnatvān nāmanāminoḥ  RBhrs ataḥ śrīkṛṣṇanāmādi na bhaved grāhyaṃ indriyaiḥ sevonmukhe hi jihvādau svayam eva sphuraty adaḥ  RBhrs   atha śrīmathurāmaṇḍale sthitiḥyathā pādmeanyeṣu puṇyatīrtheṣu muktir eva mahāphalam muktaiḥ prārthyā harer bhaktir mathurāyāṃ tu labhyate  RBhrs trivargadā kāmināṃ yā mumukṣūṇāṃ ca mokṣadā bhaktīcchor bhaktidā kas tāṃ mathurāṃ nāśrayed budhaḥ  RBhrs aho madhupurī dhanyā vaikuṇṭhāc ca garīyasī dinam ekaṃ nivāsena harau bhaktiḥ prajāyate  RBhrs durūhādbhutavīrye smin śraddhā dūre stu pañcake yatra svalpo pi sambandhaḥ saddhiyāṃ bhāvajanmane  RBhrs tatra śrīmurtiḥ yathāsmerāṃ bhaṅgītrayaparicitāṃ sācivistīrṇadṛṣṭiṃvaṃśīnyastādharakiśalayām ujjvalāṃ candrakeṇa govindākhyāṃ haritanum itaḥ keśitīrthopakaṇṭhemā prekṣiṣṭhās tava yadi sakhe bandhusange sti raṅgaḥ  RBhrs śrībhāgavataṃ yathāśaṅke nītāḥ sapadi daśamaskandhapadyāvalīnāṃvarṇāḥ karṇādhvani pathi katāmānupurvyād bhavadbhiḥ haṃho dimbhāḥ paramaśubhadān hanta dharmārthakāmānyad garhantaḥ sukhamayam amī mokṣam apy ākṣipanti  RBhrs kṛṣṇabhakto yathādṛgambhobhir dhautaḥ pulakapatalī maṇḍitatanuḥskhalann antaḥphullo dadhad atipṛthuṃ vepathum api dṛśoḥ kakṣāṃ yāvan mama sa puruṣaḥ ko py upayayauna jāte kiṃ tāvan matir iha gṛhe nābhiramate  RBhrs nāma yathāyadavadhi mama śītā vaiṇikenānugītāśrutipatham aghaśatror nāmāgāthā prayātā anavakalitapūrvāṃ hanta kām apy avasthāṃtadavadhi dadhadantarmānasaṃ śāmyatīva  RBhrs śrī mathurāmaṇḍalaṃ yathātaṭabhuvi kṛtakāntiḥ śyāmalā yās taṭinyāḥsphuṭitanavakadambālambikūjaddvirephā niravadhimadhurimṇā maṇḍiteyaṃ kathaṃ memanasi kam api bhāvaṃ kānanaśrīs tanoti  RBhrs alaukikapadārthānām acintyā śaktir īdṛśī bhāvaṃ tadviṣayaṃ cāpi yā sahaiva prakāśayet  RBhrs keṣāṃcit kvacid aṅgānāṃ yat kṣudraṃ śrūyate phalaṃ bahirmukhapravṛttyaitat kintu mukhyaṃ phalaṃ ratiḥ  RBhrs saṃmataṃ bhaktivijñānāṃ bhaktyaṅgatvaṃ na karmaṇām  RBhrs yatha caikādaśe tāvat karmāṇi kurvīta na nirvidyeta yāvatā matkathāśravaṇādau vā śraddhā yāvan na jāyate  RBhrs jñānavairāgyayor bhaktipraveśāyopayogitā īṣat prathamam eveti nāṅgatvam ucitaṃ tayoḥ  RBhrs yad ubhe cittakāṭhinyahetū prāyaḥ satāṃ mate sukumārasvabhāveyaṃ bhaktis taddhetur īritā  RBhrs yathā tatraiva tasmān madbhaktiyuktasya yogino vai madātmanaḥ na jñānaṃ na ca vairāgyaṃ prāyaḥ śreyo bhaved iha  RBhrs kintu jñānaviraktyādisādhyaṃ bhaktyaiva sidhyati  RBhrs yathā tatraiva yat karmabhir yat tapasā jñānavairāgya taś ca yat yogena dāna dharmeṇa śreyobhir itarair api  RBhrs sarvaṃ madbhaktiyogena madbhakto labhate njasā svargāpavargaṃ maddhāma kathañcid yadi vāñchati  RBhrs rucim udvahatas tatra janasya bhajane hareḥ viṣayeṣu gariṣṭho pi rāgaḥ prāyo vilīyate  RBhrs anāsaktasya viṣayān yathārham upayuñjataḥ nirbandhaḥ kṛṣṇasambandhe yuktaṃ vairāgyam ucyate  RBhrs prāpañcikatayā buddhyā harisambandhivastunaḥ mumukṣubhiḥ parityāgo vairāgyaṃ phalgu kathyate  RBhrs proktena lakṣaṇenaiva bhaktir adhikṛtasya ca aṅgatve suniraste pi nityādyakhilakarmaṇāṃ  RBhrs jnānasyādhyātmikasyāpi vairagyasya ca phalgunaḥ spaṣṭatārthaṃ punar api tad evedaṃ nirākṛtaṃ  RBhrs dhanaśiṣyādibhir dvārair yā bhaktir upapādyate vidūratvād uttamatāhānyā tasyāś ca nāṅgatā  RBhrs viśeṣaṇatvam evaiṣāṃ adbhutā vyādha tavāhiṃsādayo guṇāḥ haribhaktau pravṛttā ye na te syuḥ paratāpinaḥ  RBhrs tatraivaantaḥśuddhir bahiḥśuddhis tapaḥśāntyadayas tathā amī guṇāḥ prapadyante harisevābhikāminām  RBhrs sā bhaktir ekamukhyāṇgāśritānaikāṅgi kātha vā svavāsanānusāreṇa niṣṭhātaḥ siddhikṛd bhavet  RBhrs tatra ekāṅgāyathā granthāntare Padyāvalī  Anonymousśrī viṣṇoḥ śravaṇe parīkṣid abhavad vaiyāsakiḥ kīrtaneprahlādaḥ smaraṇe tadaṅghribhajane lakṣmīḥ pṛthuḥ pūjane akrūras tv abhivandane kapipatir dāsye tha sakhye rjunaḥsarvasvātmanivedane balir abhūt kṛṣṇāptir eṣāṃ parā  RBhrs anekāṅgā yathā navame sa vai manaḥ kṛṣṇapadāravindayorvacāṃsi vaikuṇṭhaguṇānuvarṇane karau harer mandiramārjanādiṣuśrutiṃ cakārācyutasatkathodaye  RBhrs mukundaliṅgālayadarśane dṛśautadbhṛtyagātrasparśe ṅgasaṅgamam ghrāṇaṃ ca tatpādasarojasaurabheśrīmattulasyā rasanāṃ tadarpite  RBhrs pādau hareḥ kṣetrapadānusarpaṇeśiro hṛṣīkeśapadābhivandane kāmaṃ ca dāsye na tu kāmakāmyayāyathottamaḥślokajanāśraya ratiḥ  RBhrs śāstroktayā prabalayā tattanmaryādayānvitā vaidhi bhaktir iyaṃ kaiścan maryādāmārga ucyate  RBhrs atha rāgānugāvirājantīm abhivyaktāṃ vrajavāsī janādiṣu rāgātmikām anusṛtā yā sā rāgānugocyate  RBhrs rāgānugāvivekārtham ādau rāgātmikocyate  RBhrs iṣṭe svārasikī rāgaḥ paramāviṣṭatā bhavet tanmayī yā bhaved bhaktiḥ sātra rāgātmikoditā  RBhrs sā kāmarūpā sambandharūpā ceti bhaved dvidhā  RBhrs tathā hi saptame kāmād dveṣād bhayāt snehād yathā bhaktyeśvare manaḥ āveśya tad aghaṃ hitvā bahavas tadgatiṃ gatāḥ  RBhrs gopyaḥ kāmād bhayāt kaṃso dveṣāc caidyādayo nṛpāḥ sambandhād vṛṣṇayaḥ snehād yūyaṃ bhaktyā vayaṃ vibho  RBhrs iti ānukūlyaviparyāsād bhītidveṣau parāhatau snehasya sakhyavācitvād vaidhabhaktyanuvartitā  RBhrs kiṃ vā premābhidhāyitvān nopayogo tra sādhane bhaktyā vayam iti vyaktaṃ vaidhī bhaktir udīritā  RBhrs yadarīṇāṃ priyāṇāṃ ca prāpyam ekam ivoditam tad brahmakṛṣṇayor aikyāt kiraṇārkopamājuṣoḥ  RBhrs brahmaṇy eva layaṃ yānti prāyeṇa ripavo hareḥ kecit prāpyāpi sārūpyābhāsaṃ aṅghripadmasudhāḥ premarūpās tasya priyā janāḥ  RBhrs tathā hi śrīdaśame nibhṛtamarunmano kṣadṛḍhayogayujo hṛdi yanmunaya upāsate tadarayo pi yayuḥ smaraṇāt striya uragendrabhogabhujadaṇḍaviṣaktadhiyovayam api te samāḥ samadṛśo ṅghrisarojasudhāḥ  RBhrs tatra rūpāsā kāmarūpā sambhogatṛṣṇāṃ yā nayati svatām yad asyāṃ kṛṣṇasaukhyārtham eva kevalam udyamaḥ  RBhrs iyaṃ tu vrajadevīṣu suprasiddhā virājate āsāṃ premaviśeṣo yaṃ prāptaḥ kām api mādhurīṃ tattatkrīḍānidānatvāt kāma ity ucyate budhaiḥ  RBhrs tathā ca tantrepremaiva goparāmāṇāṃ kāma ity agamat prathām  RBhrs ity uddhavādayo py etaṃ vāñchati bhagavatpriyāḥ  RBhrs kāmaprāyā ratiḥ kintu kubjāyām eva sammatā  RBhrs tatra sambandharūpāsambandharūpā govinde pitṛtvādyābhimānitā atropalakṣaṇatayā vṛṣṇīnāṃ vallavā matāḥ yadaiśyajñānaśūnyatvād eṣāṃ rāge pradhānatā  RBhrs kāmasambandharūpe te premamātrasvarūpake nityasiddhāśrayatayā nātra samyag vicārite  RBhrs rāgātmikāyā dvaividhyād dvidhā rāgānugā ca apekṣate nātra śāstraṃ na yuktiṃ ca tallobhotpattilakṣaṇam  RBhrs vaidhabhaktyadhikārī tu bhāvāvirbhavanāvadhi atra śāstraṃ tathā tarkam anukūlam apekṣate  RBhrs kṛṣṇaṃ smaran janaṃ cāsya preṣṭhaṃ yāny aṅgāni ca tāny atra vijñeyāni manīṣibhiḥ  RBhrs tatra kāmānugākāmānugā bhavet tṛṣṇā kāmarūpānugāminī  RBhrs sambhogecchāmayī tattadbhāvecchātmeti sā dvidhā  RBhrs kelitātparyavaty eva sambhogecchāmayī bhavet tadbhāvecchātmikā tāsām bhāvamādhuryakāmitā  RBhrs śrīmūrter mādhurīṃ prekṣya tattallīlāṃ niśamya vā tadbhāvākāṇkṣiṇo ye syus teṣu sādhanatānayoḥ purāṇe śruyate pādme puṃsam api bhaved iyam  RBhrs yathāpurā maharṣayaḥ sarve daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinaḥ dṛṣṭvā rāmaṃ hariṃ tatra bhoktum aicchan suvigraham  RBhrs te sarve strītvam āpannāḥ samudbhūtāś ca gokule hariṃ samprāpya kāmena RBhrs yathāvidhuritavadanā vidūnabhāsastam aghaharaṃ gahane gaveṣayantaḥ mṛdukalamuralīṃ niśamya śailevrajaśiśavaḥ pulakojjvalā babhūvuḥ  RBhrs atra viṣādaśāntiḥ śabdārtharasavaicitrī vāci kācana nāsti me yathākathañcid evoktaṃ bhāvodāharaṇaṃ param  RBhrs trayastriṃśad ime ṣṭau ca vakṣyante sthāyinaś ca ye mukhyabhāvābhidhās tv ekacatvāriṃśad amī smṛtāḥ  RBhrs śarīrendriyavargasya vikāraṇāṃ vidhāyakāḥ bhāvāvirbhāvajanitāś cittavṛttaya īritāḥ  RBhrs kvacit svābhāviko bhāvaḥ kaścid āgantukaḥ kvacit yas tu svābhāviko bhāvaḥ sa vyāpyāntarbahiḥsthitaḥ  RBhrs mañjiṣṭhādye yathā dravye rāgas tanmaya īkṣyate atra syān nāmamātreṇa vibhāvasya vibhāvatā  RBhrs etena sahajenaiva bhāvenānugatā ratiḥ ekarūpāpi yā bhakter vividhā pratibhāty asau  RBhrs āgantukas tu yo bhāvaḥ paṭādau raktimeva saḥ tais tair vibhāvair evāyaṃ dhīyate dīpyate pi ca  RBhrs vibhāvanādivaiśiṣṭyād bhaktānāṃ bhedatas tathā prāyeṇa sarvabhāvānāṃ vaiśiṣṭyam upajāyate  RBhrs vividhānāṃ tu bhaktānāṃ vaiśiṣṭyād vividhaṃ manaḥ mano nusārād bhāvānāṃ tāratamyaṃ kilodaye  RBhrs citte gariṣṭhe gambhīre mahiṣṭhe karkaśādike samyagunmīlitāś cāmī na lakṣyante sphuṭaṃ janaiḥ  RBhrs citte laghiṣṭhe cottāne kṣodiṣṭhe komalādike manāgunmīlitāś cāmī lakṣyante bahir ulbaṇāḥ  RBhrs gariṣṭhaṃ svarṇapiṇḍābhaṃ laghiṣṭhaṃ tulapiṇḍavat cittayugme tra vijñayā bhāvasya pavanopamā  RBhrs gambhīraṃ sindhuvac cittam uttānaṃ palvalādivat cittadvaye tra bhāvasya mahādriśikharopamā  RBhrs pattanābhaṃ mahiṣṭhaṃ syāt kṣodiṣṭhaṃ tu kuṭiravat cittayugme tra bhāvasya dīpenebhena vopamā  RBhrs karkaśaṃ trividhaṃ proktaṃ vajraṃ svarṇaṃ tathā jatu cittatraye tra bhāvasya jñeyā vaiśvānaropamā  RBhrs atyantakaṭhinaṃ vajram akutaścana mārdavam īdṛśaṃ tāpasādīnāṃ cittaṃ tāvad avekṣyate  RBhrs svarṇaṃ dravati bhāvāgnes tāpenātigarīyasā jatu dravatvam āyāti tāpaleśena sarvataḥ  RBhrs komalaṃ ca tridhaivoktaṃ madanaṃ navanītakam amṛtaṃ ceti bhāvo tra prāyaḥ sūryātapāyate  RBhrs draved atrādyayugalam ātapena yathāyatham dravībhūtaṃ svabhāvena sarvadaivāmṛtaṃ bhavet govindapreṣṭhavaryāṇāṃ cittaṃ syād amṛtaṃ kila  RBhrs kṛṣṇabhaktiviśeṣasya gariṣṭhatvādibhir guṇaiḥ samavetaṃ sadāmībhir dvitrair api mano bhavet  RBhrs kintu suṣṭhu RBhrs tatra saṅkulāeṣāṃ dvayos trayāṇāṃ vā sannipātas tu saṅkulā udbhavādau ca bhīmādau mathurādau krameṇa sā yasyādhikyaṃ bhaved yatra sa tena vyapadiśyate  RBhrs atha prītiḥsvasmād bhavanti ye nirvedādayo bhāvās te tu sañcāriṇo matāḥ  RBhrs eteṣāṃ tu tathābhāve bhagavatkāvyanāṭyayoḥ sevām āhuḥ paraṃ hetuṃ kecit tatpakṣarāgiṇaḥ  RBhrs kintu tatra sudustarkamādhuryādbhutasampadaḥ rater asyāḥ prabhāvo yaṃ bhavet kāraṇam uttamam  RBhrs mahāśaktivilāsātmā bhāvo cintyasvarūpabhāk ratyākhyā ity ayaṃ yukto na hi tarkeṇa bādhitum bhāratādyuktir eṣā hi prāktanair apy udāhṛtā  RBhrs yathoktam udyamaparvaṇi mabhā acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvā na tāṃs tarkeṇa yojayetprakṛtibhyaḥ paraṃ yac ca tad acintyasya lakṣaṇam  RBhrs vibhāvatādīn ānīya kṛṣṇādīn mañjulā ratiḥ etair eva tathābhūtaiḥ svaṃ saṃvardhayati sphuṭam  RBhrs yathā svair eva salilaiḥ paripūrya balāhakān ratnālayo bhavaty ebhir vṛṣṭais tair eva vāridhiḥ  RBhrs nave ratyaṅkure jāte haribhaktasya kasyacit vibhāvatvādihetutvaṃ vistīrṇāṃ kurvate ratim  RBhrs atas tasya vibhāvādicatuṣkasya rater api atra sāhāyikaṃ vyaktaṃ mitho jasram avekṣyate  RBhrs kintv etasyāḥ prabhāvo pi vairūpye sati kuñcati vairūpyas tu vibhāvāder anaucityam udīryate  RBhrs alaukikyā prakṛtyeyaṃ sudurūhā rasasthitiḥ yatra sādhāraṇatayā bhāvāḥ sādhu sphuranty amī  RBhrs eṣāṃ svaparasambandhaniyamānirṇayo hi yaḥ sādhāraṇyaṃ tad evoktaṃ bhāvānāṃ pūrvasūribhiḥ  RBhrs tad uktaṃ śrībharatenaśaktir asti vibhāvādeḥ kāpi sādhāraṇīkṛtau pramātā tadabhedena svaṃ yayā pratipadyate  RBhrs  iti duḥkhādayaḥ sphuranto pi jātu bhāntaḥ svīyatayā hṛdi prauḍhānandacamatkāracarvaṇām eva tanvate  RBhrs parāśrayatayāpy ete jātu bhāntaḥ sukhādayaḥ hṛdaye paramānandasandoham upacinvate  RBhrs sadbhāvaś ced vibhāvādeḥ kiñcinmātrasya jāyate sadyaś catuṣṭayākṣepāt pūrṇataivopapadyate  RBhrs kiṃ caratiḥ sthitānukāryeṣu laukikatvādihetubhiḥ rasaḥ syān neti nāṭyajñā yad āhur yuktam eva tat  RBhrs alaukikī tv iyaṃ kṛṣṇaratiḥ sarvādbhutādbhutā yoge rasaviśeṣatvaṃ gacchanty eva haripriye  RBhrs viyoge tv adbhutānandavivartatvaṃ dadhaty api tanoty eṣā pragāḍhārtibharābhāsatvam ūrjitā  RBhrs tatrāpi vallavādhīśanandanālambanā ratiḥ sāndrānandacamatkāraparamāvadhir iṣyate  RBhrs yatsukhaughalavāgastyaḥ pibaty eva svatejasā remaśamādhurīsākṣātkārānandābdhim apy alam  RBhrs kiṃ caparamānandatādātmyād ratyāder asya vastutaḥ rasasya svaprakāśatvam akhaṇḍatvaṃ ca sidhyati  RBhrs pūrvam uktād dvidhā bhdedān mukhyagauṇatayā rateḥ bhaved bhaktiraso py eṣa mukhyagauṇatayā dvidhā  RBhrs pañcadhāpi rater aikyān mukhyas tv eka ihoditaḥ phalguvairāgyanirdagdhāḥ śuṣkajñānāś ca haitukāḥ mīmāṃsakā viśeṣeṇa bhaktyāsvādabahirmukhāḥ  RBhrs ity eṣa bhaktirasikaś caurād iva mahānidhiḥ jaranmīmāṃsakād rakṣyaḥ kṛṣṇabhaktirasaḥ sadā  RBhrs sarvathaiva durūho yam abhaktair bhagavadrasaḥ tatpādāmbujasarvasvair bhaktair evānurasyate  RBhrs vyatītya bhāvanāvartma yaś camatkārakārabhūḥ hṛdi sattvojjvale bāḍhaṃ svadate sa raso mataḥ  RBhrs bhāvanāyāḥ pade yas tu budhenānanyabuddhinā bhāvyate gāḍhasaṃskāraiś citte bhāvaḥ sa kathyate  RBhrs gopālarūpaśobhāṃ dadhad api raghunāthabhāvavistārī tuṣyatu sanātanātmā daikṣiṇavibhāge RBhrs rasāmṛtābdher bhāge tra tṛtīye paścimābhidhe mukhyo bhaktirasaḥ pañcavidhaḥ śāntādīr īryate  RBhrs ato tra pāñcavidhyena laharyaḥ pañca kīrtitāḥ athāmī pañca lakṣyante rasāḥ śāntādayaḥ kramāt  RBhrs tatra śāntabhaktirasaḥvakṣyamāṇair vibhāvādyaiḥ śamināṃ svādyatāṃ gataḥsthāyī śāntiratir dhīraiḥ śāntabhaktirasaḥ smṛtaḥ  RBhrs prāyaḥ svasukhajātīyaṃ sukhaṃ syād atra yoginām kintv ātmasaukhyam aghanaṃ ghanaṃ tv īśam ayaṃ sukham  RBhrs tatrāpīśasvarūpānubhavasyaivoruhetutā dāsādivanmanojñatvalīlāder na tathā matā  RBhrs tatra ālambanāḥcaturbhujaś ca śāntāś ca asminn ālambanā matāḥ  RBhrs adhikṛtāśritapāriṣadānurāgāḥ  RBhrs tatra adhikṛtāḥbrahmaśaṅkaraśakrādyāḥ proktā adhikṛtā budhaiḥ rūpaṃ prasiddham evaiṣāṃ tena bhaktir udīryate  RBhrs yathākā paryety ambikeyaṃ harim avakalayan mallīkusumasukumāraḥ priyatamegariṣṭho yaṃ keśī girivad iti me vellati manaḥ śivaṃ bhūyāt paśyonnamitabhujamedhir muhur amuṃkhalaṃ kṣundan kuryāṃ vrajam atitarāṃ śālinam aham  RBhrs atra vidviṣau vīrabhayānakau vatsalaṃ puṣṇītaḥ yathākamprā svedini cūrṇakuntalataṭe ity ādi BRS   RBhrs tatra hāsyakaruṇau vatsalam eva puṣṇītaḥ api camitho vairāv api dvau yau bhāvau dharmasutādiṣu kālādibhedat prākaṭyaṃ tau vindantau na duṣyataḥ  RBhrs adhirūḍhe mahābhāve viruddhair virasāḥ yutiḥ na syād ity ujjvale rādhākṛṣṇayor darśitaṃ purā  RBhrs kvāpy acintyamahāśaktau mahāpuruṣaśekhare rasāvalisamāveśaḥ svādāyaivopajāyate  RBhrs tatra rasānāṃ viṣayatveyathā lalitamādhave daityācāryās tadāsye vikṛtim aruṇatāṃ mallavaryāḥ sakhāyogaṇḍaunnatyaṃ khaleśāḥ pralayam ṛṣigaṇā dhyānamuṣṇāsram ambāḥ romāñcaṃ sāṃyugīnāḥ kam api navacamatkāram antaḥ sureśālāsyaṃ dāsāḥ kaṭākṣaṃ yayur asitadṛśaḥ prekṣya raṅge mukundam  RBhrs āśrayatve yathāsvasmin dhūrye py amānī śiśuṣu garidhṛtāv udyateṣu smitāsyasthūtkārī dadhni visre praṇayiṣu vivṛtaprauḍhir indre ruṇākṣaḥ goṣṭhe sāśrur vidūne guruṣu harimakhaṃ prāsya kampaḥ sa pāyādāsāre sphāradṛṣṭir yuvatiṣu pulakī bibhrad adriṃ vibhur vaḥ  RBhrs iti śrīśrībhaktirasāmṛtasindhāv uttaravibhāgerasānāṃ maitrīvairasthitināmnī laharī aṣṭamī  rasābhāsākhyā navamalaharīpūrvam evānuśiṣṭena vikalā rasalakṣaṇā rasā eva rasābhāsā rasajñair anukīrtitāḥ  RBhrs syus tridhoparasāś cānurasāś cāparasāś ca te uttamā madhyamāḥ proktāḥ kaniṣṭhāś cety amī kramāt  RBhrs atra uparasāḥprāptaiḥ sthāyivibhāvānubhāvādyais tu virūpatām śāntādayo rasā eva dvādaśoparasā matāḥ  RBhrs tatra śāntoparasāḥbrahmabhāvāt parabrahmaṇy advaitādhikyayogataḥ tathā bībhatsabhūmādeḥ śānto hy uparaso bhavet  RBhrs tatra ādyaṃ yathāvijñānasuṣamādhaute samādhau yad udañcati sukhaṃ dṛṣṭe tad evādya purāṇapuruṣe tvayi  RBhrs dvitīyaṃ yathāyatra yatra viṣaye mama dṛṣṭistaṃ tam eva kalayāmi bhavantam yan nirañjana parāvarabījaṃtvāṃ vinā kim api nāparam asti  RBhrs atha prītoparasaḥkṛṣṇasyāgre tidhārṣṭyena tadbhakteṣv avahelayā svābhīṣṭadevatānyatra paramotkarṣavīkṣayā maryādātikramādyaiś ca prītoparasatā matā  RBhrs tatra ādyaṃ yathāpraṇayan vapur vivaśatāṃ satāṃ kulairavadhīryamāṇanaṭano py anargalaḥ vikira prabho dṛśam ihety akuṇṭhavākcaṭulo baṭuvyavṛṇutātmano ratim  RBhrs atha preyauparasaḥekasminn eva sakhyena harimitrādyavajñayā yuddhabhūmādinā cāpi preyānuparaso bhavet  RBhrs tatra ādyaṃ yathāsuhṛd ity udito bhiyā cakampechalito narmagirā stutiṃ cakāra sa nṛpaḥ pariripsato bhujābhyāṃhariṇā daṇḍavad agrataḥ papāta  RBhrs atha vatsaloparasaḥsāmarthyādhikyābhijñānāl lālanādyaprayatnataḥ karuṇasyātirekādes turyāś coparaso bhavet  RBhrs tatra ādyaṃ yathāmallānāṃ yadavadhi parvatodbhaṭānāmunmāthaṃ sapadi tavātmajād apaśyam nodvegaṃ tadavadhi yāmi jāmi tasmindrāghiṣṭhām api samitiṃ prapadyamāne  RBhrs atha śṛṅgāroparasaḥ tatra sthāyivairūpyamdvayor ekatarasyaiva ratir yā khalu dṛśyate yān ekatra tathaikasya sthāyinaḥ sā virūpatā vibhāvasyaiva vairūpyaṃ sthāyiny atropacaryate  RBhrs tatra ekatra ratiryathā lalitamādhavemandasmitaṃ prakṛtisiddham api vyudantaṃsaṅgopitaś ca sahajo pi dṛśos taraṅgaḥ dhūmāyite dvijavadhūmadanārtivahnāvahnāya kāpi gaitri aṅkuritām ayāsīt  RBhrs atyantābhāva evātra rateḥ khalu vivakṣitaḥ etasyāḥ prāgabhāve tu śucir noparaso bhavet  RBhrs anekatra ratir yathāgāndharvi kurvāṇam avekṣya līlāmagre dharaṇyāṃ sakhi kāmapālam ākarṇayantī ca mukundareṇuṃbhinnādya sādhvi smarato dvidhāsi  RBhrs kecit tu nāyakasyāpi sarvathā tulyarāgataḥ nāyikāsv apy anekāsu vadanty uparasaṃ śucim  RBhrs vibhāvavairūpyamvaidagdhyaujjvalyaviraho vibhāvasya virūpatā latāpaśupulindīṣu vṛddhāsv api sa vartate  RBhrs tatra latā yathāsakhi madhu kiratī niśamya vaṃśīṃmadhumathanena kaṭākṣitātha mṛdvī mukulapulakitā latāvalīyaṃratim iha pallavitāṃ hṛdi vyanakti  RBhrs paśur yathāpaśyādbhutās tuṅgamadaḥ kuraṅgīḥpataṅgakanyāpuline dya dhanyāḥ yāḥ keśavāṅge tadapāṅgapūtāḥsānaṅgaraṅgāṃ dṛśam arpayanti  RBhrs pulindī yathākālindīpuline paśya pulindī pulakācitā harer dṛkcāpalaṃ vīkṣya sahajaṃ yā vighūrṇate  RBhrs vṛddhā yathākajjalena kṛtakeśakālimābilvayugmaracitonnatastanī paśya gauri kiratī dṛgañcalaṃsmerayaty aghaharaṃ jaraty asau  RBhrs sthāyino tra virūpatvam ekarāgatayāpi cet ghaṭetāsau vibhāvasya virūpatve py udāhṛtiḥ  RBhrs śucitvaujjvalyavaidigdhyāt suveśatvāc ca kathyate śṛṅgārasya vibhāvatvam anyatrābhāsatā tataḥ  RBhrs atha anubhāvavairūpyamsamayānāṃ vyatikrāntir grāmyatvaṃ dhṛṣṭāpi ca vairūpyam anubhāvāder manīṣibhir udīritam  RBhrs tatra samayavyatikrāntiḥsamayāḥ khaṇḍitādīnāṃ priye roṣoditādayaḥ puṃsaḥ smitādayaś cātra priyayā tāḍanādiṣu eteṣām anyathābhāvaḥ samayānāṃ vyatikramaḥ  RBhrs tatra ādyaṃ yathā kāntānakhāndhito py adya parihṛtya hare hriyam kailāsavāsinīṃ dāsīṃ kṛpādṛṣṭyā bhajasva mām  RBhrs atha grāmyatvam bālaśabdādyupanyāso virasoktiprapañcanam kaṭīkaṇḍūtir ity ādyaṃ grāmyatvaṃ kathitaṃ budhaiḥ  RBhrs tatra ādyaṃ yathā kiṃ naḥ phaṇikiśorīṇāṃ tvaṃ puṣkarasadāṃ sadā muralīdhvaninā nīvīṃ gopabāla vilumpasi  RBhrs atha dhṛṣṭatāprakaṭaprārthanādiḥ syāt sambhogādes tu dhṛṣṭatā  RBhrs yathākānta kailāsakuñjo yaṃ ramyāhaṃ navayauvanā tvaṃ vidagdho si govinda kiṃ vā vācyam ataḥ param  RBhrs evam eva tu gauṇānāṃ hāsādīnām api svayam vijñeyoparasatvasya manīṣibhir udāhṛtiḥ  RBhrs atha anurasāḥbhaktādibhir vibhāvādyaiḥ kṛṣṇasambandhavarjitaiḥ rasā hāsyādayaḥ sapta śāntaś cānurasā matāḥ  RBhrs tatra hāsyānurasaḥtāṇḍavaṃ vyadhita hanta kakkhaṭīmarkaṭī bhrūkuṭībhis tathoddhuram yena vallavakadambakaṃ babhauhāsaḍambarakarambitānanam  RBhrs atha adbhutānurasaḥbhāṇḍīrakakṣe bahudhā vitaṇḍāṃvedāntatantre śukamaṇḍalasya ākarṇayan nirnimiṣākṣipakṣmāromāñcitāṅgaś ca surarṣir āsīt  RBhrs evam evātra vijñeyā vīrāder apy udāhṛtiḥ  RBhrs aṣṭāv amī taṭastheṣu prākaṭyaṃ yadi bibhrati kṛṣṇādibhir vibhāvādyair gatair anubhavādhvani  RBhrs atha aparasāḥkṛṣṇatatpratipakṣaś ced viṣayāśrayatāṃ gatāḥ hāsādīnāṃ tadā te tra prājñair aparasā matāḥ  RBhrs tatra hāsyāparasaḥpalāyamānam udvīkṣya capalāyatalocanam kṛṣṇam ārāj jarāsandhaḥ solluṇṭham ahasīn muhuḥ  RBhrs evam anye pi vijñeyās te dbhutāparasādayaḥ uttamās tu rasābhāsāḥ kaiścid rasatayoditāḥ  RBhrs tathā hibhāvāḥ sarve tadābhāsā rasābhāsāś ca kecana amī proktarasābhijñaiḥ sarve pi rasanād rasāḥ  RBhrs bhāratādyāś catasras tu rasāvasthānasūcikāḥ vṛttayo nāṭyamātṛtvād uktā nāṭakalakṣaṇe  RBhrs granthasya gauravabhayād asyā bhaktirasaśriyaḥ samāhṛtiḥ samāsena mayā seyaṃ vinirmitā gopālarūpaśobhāṃ dadhad api raghunāthabhāvavisārī tuṣyatu sanātano sminn uttarabhāge rasāmṛtāmbhodheḥ iti śrīśrībhaktirasāmṛtasindhāv uttaravibhāgerasābhāsalaharī navamī iti śrīśrībhaktirasāmṛtasindhau gauṇabhaktirasanirūpaṇo nāma caturtho vibhāgaḥ samāptaḥ rāmāṅgaśatrugaṇite śāke gokulam adhiṣṭhitenāyam bhaktirasāmṛtasindhur viṭaṅkitaḥ kṣudrarūpeṇa samāpto yaṃ śrīśrībhaktirasāmṛtasindhuḥ Thank you for using a Gaudiya
